1.Why do penny stock companies reverse split their stock?
Companies, especially the small caps, become publicly listed to raise money from investors. Most penny stocks are vehicles for inside shareholders to dilute and hence generate cash flow as ATM offerings.
So these stocks try very hard to stay listed on Nasdaq, to do so they must keep $1 bid minimum. That's why these stocks reverse split to reduce their share price, and tighten up their float outstanding. So the stock becomes easier to be bid up when they conveniently release PR after the reverse split is finished!
That's why we see $VIVE release PR, and Goldman Sachs scooping up some common shares just days after their 1 for 100 reverse split. Someone's definitely making money from this pump, just not the investors.

2. How to find reverse split penny stocks to trade EARLY?
I personally use Benzinga pro to screen for recent reverse split stocks that released PR with headline keywords such as "reverse split", "delisting", and "offering". That tells me that these stocks are struggling to stay compliance with Nasdaq, and will do something soon to pump their stock up after the reverse split is finished.

3.How to buy penny stocks early?
Theres plenty of money to be made by waking up early. Benzinga pro sends live email alerts whenever the penny stocks I'm tracking release a PR headline, files SEC filing etc. So I already know what to do when I see volume trading above average premarket on $VIVE. I know the support to buy the dips and sell at highs near premarket before dilution happens at the opening spike.

Penny Stock Market Cycles Explained - penny stock trading for beginners 2020

* Don't rely on patterns, trade the traders
* Low float gap ups are likely to hold
1. Long premarket break & hold
2. Buy the downtrend break after a consolidation period.
1) Check the time of the day
2) Check the volume
3) Don't buy breakouts
* Either you take action in the morning push or you get in after the midday consolidation with the downtrend break.
3. Swing strong closers overnight
* Short day 2 or 3

# Buyer's market:
Longs - day 1 multiple upsides, possible day 2 & 3
Shorts - day 1 scalps, wait for day 2 & 3 short

# Seller's market:
Longs - day 1 early scalps, no play day 2 & 3
Shorts - day 1 short all day fade, possible day 2 & 3

How to read SEC Filings - Penny stock offerings $NERV

* A shelf offering is a Securities and Exchange Commission(SEC) provision that allows an issuer to register a new issue security without selling the entire issue at once. The issuer can sell portions of the issue over a three-year period without reregistering the security or incurring penalties. A shelf offering is also known as a shelf registration.

An at-the-market(ATM) offering is a type of follow-on offering of stock utilized by publicly traded companies in order to raise capital over time. The broker-dealer sells the issuing company's shares in the open market and receives cash proceeds from the transaction.

* ATM Underwriters(dangerous signal)
-> Jefferies
-> Maxim
-> H.C. Wainwright


5 KEY Lessons to Day Trading Penny Stocks ( Low float stocks $SOLY $ELTK $GNCA $DMPI )

1. Low floats running on day 1 with fresh news = long on dips
2. Swing strong day 1 mover overnight
3. Scan for recent reverse split stocks
4. Stop buying breakouts
-> bad risk reward
-> work best in morning with strong volume
-> buy downtrend break instead
5. Take the meat of the move, avoid mid day grind, avoid MM(market maker) manipulation

* Use higher timeframe 5min or 10 min
-> helps with patience
-> bigger picture
-> avoid dead grind

* When there are too many stocks popping, momentum dies
-> buying volume is too spread out
* Do your own DD. Check float, news, enter on dips.
* Swing strong day 1 movers overnight
* Scan for reverse split stocks
* Do not buy breakouts
* Avoid mid day grind and MM manipulation

* Reverse split
1. To maintain $1 bid price to meet exchange compliance
2. To stay attractive to potential investors
3. To tighten stock float

* Micro float: 800,000 shares


Intro to Penny Stock Trading Psychology - Day trading for beginners ($ABIO Stock)

1. Breakout traders
-> most predictable traders
-> most commonly taught strategies
2. Momentum traders
-> buy strength
3. Dip guyers
-> buy strong stocks on pull backs
4. Swing traders
-> overnight swing traders buy stocks closing strong
5. Short sellers
-> enter on extensions
-> some traders love to short anything that's "up too much"

* Forget patterns, understand trader psychology
* Chart patterns are psychological decisions to buy or sell
* Don't trade patterns, trade the traders

How to Day Trade and Buy Penny Stock Gappers and Gaps - Beginner Day Trading Strategy

Penny stock gap up - long set up

# 3 Criteria
1. Confirmed deal with major company
-> Likely to hold the gap & break out highter
-> worth a swing trade
2. Low float
Float -> amount of shares outstanding
Low float -> 2-3 million or less(finvis.com)
-> not enough supply to meet the demand
-> causes short squeeze & float rotation
3. High short interest
+25%(shortsqueeze.com)
>>> 2 + 3 = Short squeeze!(to the moon)

Do not buy penny stock break outs
Plan out your entries with good risk reward(1:3 or better)
Day trading -> timing and entry
With penny stocks, you could be fundamentally right but technically wrong.
-> be very selective and very patient
